9:00 AM

remote meeting by interactive conference technology, via BlueJeans 
https://maui.bluejeans.com/295235670.

Floor, 200 S. High Street, Wailuku, Hawaii.

TIME MEETING ADJOURNED: 2:59 a.m. 
We're on the air. OK, OK, OK, good morning, members, And good morning. 
Are our people in the gallery? Seven twenty twenty three will now come to 
order. And this clerk will you please proceed with call starting from 
right to left? Good morning, everyone. Chair proceeding with roll call 
members participating from non-public locations should state who, if 
anyone except minors is present with them as part of Good Morning. And 
it's great to see all of you. Councilmember Yuki Sukumaran. Good morning. 
And yes, I agree. It's great to be back in the chambers. Councilmember 
Tamara Paltin, Aloha Academy Cockerel. Broadcasting live in direct from 
rainy old Hilo Town. And with me, I have Mildred and Samuel Paltin. Sorry 
to not be in the chambers with you all. My mother had a stroke last 
Friday, but she's doing great. And thank you so much. Councilmember Gabe 
Johnson. Morning, everyone. I'm happy to be here and ready to aloha, 
a.k.a. Jeremiah Maui Nui Yakama. Today is an exciting day for our 
meeting, of course, and I'm A. Again, so congratulations to my brother, 
Councilmember Tom Cook, Good morning. Or like all, I'm happy to be here 
and looking little time to you. Recharge the water, Marty. Happy birthday 
to my grandma and Nancy. I share and cookie for you. I don't know how to 
put them on you before I the see you would please act as our
